TMNetsim may be deployed on any PC with a Microsoft OS supporting MSIX:\r\n* A stand-alone PC.\r\n* The Client PC end of a communication protocol.\r\n* The Server PC end of a communication protocol.\r\nTMNetsim is primarily used to simulate network delay, however, in some cases it may be used to simulate packet loss or out-of-order delivery, as well as packet capture.  Settings to control delivery delay and loss may be set on a global basis or per conversation basis.  These parameters may also be set in a per-direction basis.  A monitor allows you to view current conversations, and you may select specific instances to modify parameters for that connection on-the-fly.\r\nTMNetsim works with most all TCP socket based protocols, including FTP, RDP, and ICA.  To work with any arbitrary protocol all you need to know is the TCP Socket that the server listens to.  Loss and out-of-order delivery, when set too large, will cause most TCP protocols to fail, so it should be used with caution.  Only when the application protocol provides additional flow control or sequencing at a higher layer is use of Loss and OOO possible above a couple of percent.","ProductFamilyName":"Apps","Schema":"Card;1"}],"Title":"Most popular","HasThirdPartyIAPs":false,"AlgoName":"RECO-Algo-Version","AlgoValue":"Lists;mostPopular;;Apps;00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000003","TotalItems":990,"PageSize":200}}
